    # ID, N_Days, Status, Drug, Age, Sex, Ascites, Hepatomegaly, Spiders, Edema, Bilirubin, Cholesterol, Albumin, Copper, Alk_Phos, SGOT, Tryglicerides, Platelets, Prothrombin, Stage

```python
import pandas as pd

# Generate 10 patient records
records = pd.DataFrame(
    np.arange(1, 11).repeat(2),
    index=np.arange(1, 11),
    columns=[
        "ID", "N_Days", "Status", "Drug", "Age", "Sex", "Ascites", "Hepatomegaly", "Spiders", "Edema", "Bilirubin", "Cholesterol", "Albumin", "Copper", "Alk_Phos", "SGOT", "Tryglicerides", "Platelets", "Prothrombin", "Stage"
    ]
)

# Populate the data with realistic values
records["Drug"] = np.random.choice(["D-penicillamine", "Placebo"])
records["Age"] = np.random.randint(18, 80)
records["Sex"] = np.random.choice(["F", "M"])
records["Ascites"] = np.random.choice(["Y", "N"])
records["Hepatomegaly"] = np.random.choice(["Y", "N"])
records["Spiders"] = np.random.choice(["Y", "N"])
records["Edema"] = np.random.choice(["N", "S", "Y"])
records["Bilirubin"] = np.random.randint(0, 20)
records["Cholesterol"] = np.random.randint(100, 400)
records["Albumin"] = np.random.randint(2, 4)
records["Copper"] = np.random.randint(0, 20)
records["Alk_Phos"] = np.random.randint(50, 150)
records["SGOT"] = np.random.randint(50, 200)
records["Tryglicerides"] = np.random.randint(0, 100)
records["Platelets"] = np.random.randint(50, 200)
records["Prothrombin"] = np.random.randint(10, 20)
records["Stage"] = np.random.randint(1, 4)

# Print the generated records
print(records)
```

```python
# Generate realistic patient records for liver cirrhosis research

# Define the number of records to generate
num_records = 10

# Generate records
patient_records = []

# For each record...
for i in range(num_records):
    # Create a patient record
    patient_record = {
        "ID": i,
        "N_Days": random.randint(1, 10),
        "Status": ["C", "CL", "D"][random.randint(0, 2)],
        "Drug": ["D-penicillamine", "Placebo"][random.randint(0, 1)],
        "Age": random.randint(18, 80),
        "Sex": ["F", "M"][random.randint(0, 1)],
        "Ascites": ["Y", "N"][random.randint(0, 1)],
        "Hepatomegaly": ["Y", "N"][random.randint(0, 1)],
        "Spiders": ["Y", "N"][random.randint(0, 1)],
        "Edema": ["N", "S", "Y"][random.randint(0, 2)],
        "Bilirubin": random.randint(0, 20),
        "Cholesterol": random.randint(100, 300),
        "Albumin": random.uniform(2.0, 4.0),
        "Copper": random.randint(10, 20),
        "Alk_Phos": random.randint(50, 150),
        "SGOT": random.randint(50, 200),
        "Tryglicerides": random.randint(0, 100),
        "Platelets": random.randint(50, 200),
        "Prothrombin": random.randint(10, 20),
        "Stage": random.randint(1, 4)
    }

    # Add the patient record to the list
    patient_records.append(patient_record)

# Print the patient records
print(patient_records)
```

4. Drug is either D-penicillamine or Placebo
5. Ensure values fall within medically reasonable ranges

Features:

1. ID: Patient ID

5. Age: Patient's age in days  
6. Sex: F or M  
7. Ascites: Y or N  
8. Hepatomegaly: Y or N

10. Edema: N=no, S=slight, Y=marked  
11. Bilirubin: mg/dL  
12. Cholesterol: mg/dL  
13. Albumin: g/dL  
14. Copper: µg/dL  
15. Alk_Phos: alkaline phosphatase (U/L)  
16. SGOT: aspartate aminotransferase (U/L)  
17. Tryglicerides: mg/dL  
18. Platelets: count (×1000/mm³)  
19. Prothrombin: seconds  
20. Stage: histologic stage (1-4)
